<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зацепивший.html>зацепи́вший</a> (8295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепивший.html>зацепи́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zacepívšij</span>)

***зацепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зацепить.html>зацепи́ть</a> (8295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цепи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-cepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цеплять.html>цепля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cepljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, constructed as if derived from <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*цепи́ть</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепить.html>зацепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zacepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зацепля́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цеплять.html>цепля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hook, to grapple, to fasten</li>
<li>to catch (accidentally)</li></ol>

***зацепиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зацепиться.html>зацепи́ться</a> (7363)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепить.html>зацепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zacepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепиться.html>зацепи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zacepítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зацепля́ться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цепляться.html>цепля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепиться.html>зацепи́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гвоздь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">palʹtó <b>zacepílosʹ</b> za gvozdʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the coat caught on a nail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch hold <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to catch <i>(at)</i>, to grab <i>(at)</i>, to snatch <i>(at)</i>, to seize <i>(on)</i>, to fasten <i>(onto)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go <i>(by)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепиться.html>зацепи́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">né za što <b>zacepítʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is nothing to go by; there is no clue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зацепить.html>зацепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zacepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***зачастить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачастить.html>зачасти́ть</a> (13509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частить.html>части́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">častítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачастить.html>зачасти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">začastítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to quicken
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зачастить.html>зачасти́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ <b>začastíl</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it began to rain harder; the rain began to pelt down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пульс</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зачастить.html>зачасти́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pulʹs <b>začastíl</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">smb's pulse quickened/raced</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to begin to clatter/batter/chug</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk at a great speed, to spout words</li>
<li>to become a frequent visitor <i>(to a place)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зачастить.html>зачасти́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on k nam <b>začastíl</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he's become a frequent/regular visitor here; he visits us far more often now</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачатие.html>зача́тие</a> (25026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачать.html>зача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">začátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачатие.html>зача́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">začátije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачатие.html>зача́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачатие.html>зача́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачатие.html>зача́тий</a></b>)
</p>

***зачем.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a> (249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of the phrase <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za čem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, instrumental singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">what</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This was originally marked as Saint Petersburg dialect, while in Moscow <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зачто́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaštó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was used as late as the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">začém</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative adverb</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> why? <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with what object/for what purpose</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">začém</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> differs from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">počemú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in that the latter simply means, "Why?" while <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">začém</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means, "What for?" Sometimes the words are interchangeable, but sometimes one is more appropriate than the other.</li>
<li>The reply begins with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štóby</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затем.html>зате́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatém, štóby</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заче́м-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">začém-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лью</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">― <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a>! ― <a href = vnd.unilang:воскликнуть.html>воскли́кнул</a> Воланд, ― <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позолотить.html>позолоти́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усы́</a>? </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причина.html>причи́не</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отчего.html>отчего</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">― <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>така́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бка</a>! ― <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маргарит.html>Маргари́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зимо́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>си́дя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печка.html>пе́чки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>глядя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a>, ― <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тогда.html>тогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>ушла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a>? </span></li>
</ul></li>

***зачеркнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачеркнуть.html>зачеркну́ть</a> (14522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черкнуть.html>черкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čerknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачеркнуть.html>зачеркну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">začerknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зачёркивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cross out, to strike out, to strike off, to strike through</li>
<li>to efface, to reduce to nothing, to cancel out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зачеркнуть.html>зачеркну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:достигнутый.html>дости́гнутое</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>začerknútʹ</b> dostígnutoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cancel out the result(s) achieved</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зачеркнуть.html>зачеркну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>začerknútʹ</b> istóriju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deny/discredit history</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***зачерпнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачерпнуть.html>зачерпну́ть</a> (13128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">черпну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čerpnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачерпнуть.html>зачерпну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">začerpnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачерпывать.html>заче́рпывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw, to scoop, to spoon up/out, to ladle out</li>
<li>to take in, to ship <i>(water)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накрениться.html>накрени́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зачерпнуть.html>зачерпну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódka nakrenílasʹ i <b>začerpnúla</b> vodý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat heeled over and shipped [took in / on] water</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачет.html>зачёт</a> (10106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачет.html>зачёт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">začót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачет.html>зачёта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачет.html>зачёты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачет.html>зачётов</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance<span class="ib-comma">,</span> trade</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> setoff, offset</li>
<li>pass (of a task, test)</li>
